remarks:        BGP Community Strings
remarks:        ------------------------------------------------------
remarks:        BGP Communities to control local preference inside Opentransit
remarks:        (available for BGP customers)
remarks:        ------------------------------------------------------
remarks:        Customers LP=100, Peers LP=85, Content Providers LP=150
remarks:        5511:0 Set NEXT_HOP=Null0. Traffic to host prefix is dropped
remarks:        5511:70 Set LOCAL_PREF=70 instead of default 100
remarks:        5511:80 Set LOCAL_PREF=80 instead of default 100
remarks:        5511:90 Set LOCAL_PREF=90 instead of default 100
remarks:        Default LOCAL_PREF= 100
remarks:        ------------------------------------------------------
remarks:        BGP Communties for prepend and selective prepends
remarks:        Add to AS_PATH: x=0 reject route, x=1 (5511), x=2 (5511 5511)
